	function showHide (ids,ads) {

		var oAds = $("#"+ads);
		oIds.on({

				e.stopPropagation();

		})
	}

<script type="text/javascript">
(function($) {
    var picCur = 0,
        picSum = $('.picpart_1 li').size(),
        wid;

    function changePic() {
        $('.picpart_1 li').hide();
        $('.picpart_1 li').eq(picCur).fadeTo(300, 1);
    };

    function autoPic() {
        picCur += 1;
        picCur %= picSum;
        changePic();
    };

    $('.picpart_1 li').first().show();
    $('.picpart_1 li').each(function () {
      var n = $(this).index() + 1;
        $(this).find('span').html(n + ' / ' + picSum);
    });
    $('#rarr_1').on('click', function() {
        picCur += 1;
        picCur %= picSum;
        changePic();
    });
    $('#larr_1').on('click', function() {
        picCur -= 1;
        picCur += picSum;
        picCur %= picSum;
        changePic();
    });
    wid = window.setInterval(autoPic, 5000);
    $('.picpart_1').on('mouseenter', function () {
        window.clearInterval(wid);
    }).on('mouseleave', function () {
        wid = window.setInterval(autoPic, 5000);
    });
})(jQuery);
(function($) {
  var n = $('.bg_pic').text(),
  	  s = 'url('+ n +')';
  $('.banner').css('background-image', s);
})(jQuery);
</script>
<script type="text/javascript">
(function ($) {
  //æ°é»åè¡¨å±ç¤º
  var MonthArr = ['Jan','Feb','Mar','Apr','May','Jun','Jul','Aug','Sep','Oct','Nov','Dec'];
  var curDate = new Date(),
      curYear = curDate.getFullYear(),
      curMonth = curDate.getMonth(),
      curDay = curDate.getDate(),
      starTime = {};
  var totalNumber = $('#newsList li').length,
      pageNumber = 3,
      totalPage = Math.ceil(totalNumber / pageNumber),
      curPage = 1;
  if(totalPage <= 1) {
    $('#showmore').hide();
  }
  $('#newsList li').each(function(idx) {
    if(idx >= pageNumber) {
      $(this).hide();
    }
    $(this).append('<span class="line"></span>');
    timeDispose($(this).find('.time'));
    newsStyle($(this).find('.title span'));
  });
  
  $('#showmore').on('click',function() {
    curPage++;
    $('#newsList li:lt('+ (curPage * pageNumber) +')').show();
    if(totalPage == curPage) {
      $('#showmore').hide();
    }
  });
    
  function timeDispose(obj) {
    var targetDate = new Date(obj.text()),
        targetYear = targetDate.getFullYear(),
        targetMonth = targetDate.getMonth(),
        targetDay = targetDate.getDate(),
        targetHours = targetDate.getHours(),
        targetMinutes = targetDate.getMinutes();
    if(!starTime.state) {
      starTime.month = targetDate.getMonth();
      starTime.day = targetDate.getDate();
      starTime.state = 0;
    }
    if(starTime.month != targetDate.getMonth() || starTime.day != targetDate.getDate()) {
      starTime.month = targetDate.getMonth();
      starTime.day = targetDate.getDate();
      starTime.state = 0;
    }
    
    if(curYear === targetYear && curMonth === targetMonth && curDay === targetDay) {
      if(targetMinutes < 10) {
        obj.html(targetHours + ':0' + targetMinutes);
      } else {
        obj.html(targetHours + ':' + targetMinutes);
      }
    }
    if(curYear !== targetYear || curMonth !== targetMonth || curDay !== targetDay) {
      if(starTime.month == targetMonth && starTime.day == targetDay && starTime.state == 1) {
        obj.html('&nbsp;');
      } else {
        obj.html('<span>' + targetDay + '</span>' + MonthArr[targetMonth]);
        starTime.state = 1;
      }
    }
  }
  
  function newsStyle(obj) {
    var newsStyle = $.trim(obj.text());
    if(newsStyle == 'å¤§å¾') {
      obj.addClass('bigPic').html('');
      obj.parent().siblings('.info').find('.pic img').addClass('bigPic');
    } else if(newsStyle == 'ç¬å®¶') {
      obj.addClass('exclusive').html('');
    } else {
      obj.html('');
    }
  }
})(jQuery);
</script>

var speed = 20;

var sTap = document.getElementById("scroll_cnt");

var sTap1 = document.getElementById("sn_list1");

var sTap2 = document.getElementById("sn_list2");

sTap2.innerHTML = sTap1.innerHTML;

var marqueen = function(){

	if(sTap2.offsetWidth - sTap.scrollLeft <= 0){

		sTap.scrollLeft -= sTap2.offsetWidth;

	}else{

		sTap.scrollLeft++;

	}

};

var marTimer = setInterval(marqueen,speed);

sTap.onmouseover = function(){

	clearInterval(marTimer);

}

sTap.onmouseout = function(){

	marTimer = setInterval(marqueen,speed);

}

            function Scrollimg(id) {
                $(id).find('li').first().show();
                var ImgLi = $(id).find('li');
                var ImgNum = $(id).find('.num');
                var ImgScl = $(id).find('.left');
                var ImgScr = $(id).find('.right');
                var nCur = 0;
                var wid;
                var ImgSize = $(id).find('li').size();
                $(id).find('li').each(function () {
                    ImgNum.append('<p>&nbsp;<\/p>');
                })
                ImgNum.find('p').first().addClass('cur');

                ImgNum.find('p').on('mouseenter', function () {
                    nCur = $(this).index();
                    ChangeImg(id, nCur);
                })
                ImgScr.on('click', function () {
                    nCur += 1;
                    nCur %= ImgSize;
                    ChangeImg(id, nCur);
                })
                ImgScl.on('click', function () {
                    nCur -= 1;
                    nCur += ImgSize;
                    nCur %= ImgSize;
                    ChangeImg(id, nCur);
                })

                function ChangeImg(id, idx) {
                    $(id).find('.num').find('p').removeClass('cur');
                    $(id).find('.num').find('p').eq(idx).addClass('cur');
                    $(id).find('li').hide();
                    $(id).find('li').eq(idx).show();
                }

                function autoplay() {
                    nCur += 1;
                    nCur %= ImgSize;
                    ChangeImg(id, nCur);
                }
                
                wid = window.setInterval(autoplay, 4000);
                
                $(id).on('mouseenter', function () {
                    window.clearInterval(wid);
                }).on('mouseleave', function () {
                    wid = window.setInterval(autoplay, 4000);
                })
            }
			
        })(jQuery); 
-->
